```c
// Hidden C++ exception states: #wind=166 #try_helpers=1
void __fastcall __noreturn CSetupPlatformPrivate::Execute(__int64 a1, unsigned int a2, _DWORD *a3, unsigned int *a4)
{

  int v7; // r14d
  const struct UnBCL::String *v8; // rbx

  struct UnBCL::String *v13; // rax

  struct UnBCL::String *v16; // rax
  const struct UnBCL::String *v17; // rax
  const struct UnBCL::String *v18; // rbx
  const struct UnBCL::String *v19; // rax
  struct UnBCL::String *v20; // rax
```
